With current Bitcoin Difficulty it not easy to find even share on not ASIC devices. So we DON'T RECOMMEND TO USE OUR SOFTWARE FOR PROFESSIONAL AND LONG TIME RUNNING. Advanced users can changed it.\r\n- You remain anonymous apart from your btc address.\r\n- Uses solo mining pool.
